add_namespace = WORLD
add_namespace = novel #for althist novels

# Hitler dead non hidden event
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.2"}
	title = WORLD.2.t
	desc = WORLD.2.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_adolph_hitler
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.2.a
	}
}

news_event = { # The German Civil War
	id = WORLD.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.5"}
	title = WORLD.5.t
	desc = WORLD.5.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_german_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.5.a
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = 2 }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				BRG = { TNO_BRG_domestic_tree_swap = yes }
				
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = USA }
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
}

# Anti-Heydrich Pact
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.28"}
	title = WORLD.28.t
	desc = WORLD.28.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_nuremberg_ruins

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = BGR
				original_tag = GGR
				original_tag = SGR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.b
		trigger = {
			original_tag = HGR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.c
		trigger = {
			original_tag = BRG
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.28.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = BGR
				original_tag = GGR
				original_tag = SGR
				original_tag = HGR
				original_tag = BRG
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #The Franco-Burgundian War
	id = WORLD.37
	immediate =  {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.37" }
	title = WORLD.37.t
	desc = WORLD.37.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_ss_troops

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			IBR = {
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.4101
					days = 7
				}
			}
			IBR = {
				country_event = {
					id = IBR.3213
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.37.a
		set_global_flag = france_invaded
		trigger = {
			original_tag = FRA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.37.b
		set_global_flag = france_invaded
		trigger = {
			original_tag = BRG
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.37.c
		set_global_flag = france_invaded
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = FRA
				original_tag = BRG
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = WORLD.463 #Iberia abandons the Gibraltar Dam
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.463"}
	title = WORLD.463.t
	desc = WORLD.463.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_gibraltar_dam

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.463.a #iberia
		trigger = {
			tag = IBR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.463.b #rest of the world
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
			}
		}
	}
}
news_event = {
	id = WORLD.464 #Iberian Council - Advisory
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.464"}
	title = WORLD.464.t
	desc = WORLD.464.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_council_advisory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.464.a #iberia
		trigger = {
			tag = IBR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.464.b #non far-right countries
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = socialist
				has_government = social_democracy
				has_government = liberal_democracy
				has_government = conservative_democracy
				has_government = authoritarian_democracy
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.464.c #far-right countries
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = despotism
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = esoteric_nazism
				has_government = ultranationalism
			}

		}
	}
}

news_event = { #Algerian war
	id = WORLD.915
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.915"}
	title = WORLD.915.t
	desc = WORLD.915.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_algeria_war

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.a

		trigger =  {
			original_tag = ITA
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.b

		trigger =  {
			original_tag = IBR
		}

		clr_country_flag = IBR_decisions_post_trium
		set_country_flag = IBR_decisions_foreign
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = IBR_Francisco_Franco
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {IBR_caudillo_correct_var = 1}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IBRIberiaStability
			value = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_sub_stability_small_tt

		custom_effect_tooltip = IBR_pp_foreign_get_tt

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = IBR.31051
				days = 10
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WORLD.915.c

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = ITA
					original_tag = IBR
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

news_event = { #Falangists Seize Power in Iberia
	id = WORLD.1500
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.1500"}
	title = WORLD.1500.t
	desc = WORLD.1500.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_iberia_armada_coup

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.1500.a #iberia
		trigger = {
			tag = IBR
		}
		set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.1500.b #non far-right countries
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = socialist
				has_government = social_democracy
				has_government = liberal_democracy
				has_government = conservative_democracy
				has_government = authoritarian_democracy
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WORLD.1500.c #far-right countries
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IBR
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = despotism
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = esoteric_nazism
				has_government = ultranationalism
			}

		}
	}
}

news_event = { #Göring Germany declares war on Burgundy for Fall Schwarz
	id = WORLD.14999
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.14999" }
	title = WORLD.14999.t
	desc = WORLD.14999.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_news_event_madagaskar_civil_war


	option = { #We will crush the traitors
		name = WORLD.14999.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = 65 }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}


	option = { #THe decadent fools will face their doom
		name = WORLD.14999.b
		trigger = {
			tag = BRG
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = 65 }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #The final battle is come
		name = WORLD.14999.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = esoteric_nazism
			NOT = {
				tag = BRG
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = 65 }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Oh my god!
		name = WORLD.14999.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = BRG
					tag = GER
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = communist
				has_government = ultranationalism
				has_government = national_socialism
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = conservative_democracy
				has_government = social_democracy
				has_government = liberal_democracy
				has_government = socialist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = 65 }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #The Fall of Suzuki
	id = WORLD.16600
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event WORLD.16600"}
	title = WORLD.16600.t
	desc = WORLD.16600.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_suzuki

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WORLD.16600.a
		trigger = { tag = GNG }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { GNG_general_status_var = 1 }
			GNG_update_status = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_corruption_status_var = 0 }
			GNG_update_corruption = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_fiscal_status_var = 2 }
			GNG_update_fiscal = yes
			set_variable = { GNG_kenpeitai_status_var = 2 }
			GNG_update_kenpeitai = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = despotism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.3
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = despotism
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				GNG_Matsuzawa_Takuji_hog
				GNG_Ibuka_Masaru_for
				GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_eco
			}
			add_ideas = {
				GNG_Matsushita_Masaharu_Yasuda_hog
				GNG_Morita_Akio_Yasuda_for
				GNG_Ibuka_Masaru_eco
			}
			random_list = {
				25 = { #Morita
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_PATH
							option = GNG_PATH_THE_ASCENDANT_HEIR
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_PATH
							option = GNG_PATH_THE_SILICON_VISIONARY
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						news_event = {
							id = WORLD.16601
							days = 365
						}
					}
				}
				40 = { #Matsushita
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_PATH
							option = GNG_PATH_THE_GADGETEER_OF_GUANGDONG
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_PATH
							option = GNG_PATH_THE_SILICON_VISIONARY
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						news_event = {
							id = WORLD.16602
							days = 365
						}
					}
				}
				35 = { #Ibuka
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_PATH
							option = GNG_PATH_THE_GADGETEER_OF_GUANGDONG
						}
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GNG_PATH
							option = GNG_PATH_THE_ASCENDANT_HEIR
						}
					}
					every_country = {

# INDEX
# 0 - Gorbachev Unification
# 1 - Kaminski Unification
# 2 - Saucken Unification
# 3 - Helldorff Unification
# 4 - "Chaotic" Unification

news_event = {
	id = msk_dissolution_news.0  # 0 - Gorbachev Unification
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: Dissolution - Gorbachev Unification" }
	title = msk_dissolution_news.0.t
	desc = msk_dissolution_news.0.desc
	picture = GFX_MSK_dissolution_news_RDC
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	option = {
		name = msk_dissolution_news.0.a
		trigger = { tag = RDC }
	}
	option = {
		name = msk_dissolution_news.0.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				tag = SGR
				tag = BGR
				tag = GGR
				tag = HGR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = msk_dissolution_news.0.c
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = msk_dissolution_news.0.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = GER
					tag = SGR
					tag = BGR
					tag = GGR
					tag = HGR
					tag = RDC
					tag = USA
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
